    <script type="text/javascript">
     require(['jquery'], function($) {
   		//open the search input
        $('.btn-open-search').on('click', function(evnt) {
        	$('.nav-more-wrapper').hide(); //if nav-more-wrapper is opened, must hide it

        	if ($('.search').hasClass('opened')) {
        		$('.search').removeClass('opened');
        		$(this).removeClass('opened');
				$( '.search' ).animate({ height: "0" }, 200 );
        	}else{
        		$('.search').addClass('opened');
        		$(this).addClass('opened');
				$( '.search' ).animate({ height: "96px" }, 200 );
				$('.rebelbar .search input').focus();
        	}
        });

        // This script is to stick and update the rebelbar on top
    	var target = $('body'),
    		className = 'fixed-header',
    		threshold = $('.rebelbar-before').outerHeight(true);
    	var isFixed;

    	function headerRefresh(){
    		var value = $(window).scrollTop() &gt; threshold;
            if (isFixed != value) {
            	isFixed= value;	
            	target.toggleClass(className, value);
                $('.nav-more-wrapper').hide();
                $(window).trigger('resize.submenu');
            }
    	}

        $(window).scroll(headerRefresh);
        $('.share-plus').click( function(evnt) { $('.share-buttons').toggleClass('enable-panel'); });  

        //replace the domain in native ads
        var liveDomain= "http://www.distractify.com";
        
        function replaceDomain(){
            var path= window.location.pathname;
            $('.ad-native.replacedomain').attr('data-src', liveDomain + path).removeClass('replacedomain');
        }

        if (window.location.origin != liveDomain){
            $('.infinite-scroll-wrapper').bind("DOMSubtreeModified",function(){
                replaceDomain();
            });
            replaceDomain();
        }

        headerRefresh();
    });
    </script>

        function loadChartbeat() {

            document.body.appendChild(e);
        }
        var oldonload = window.onload;
        window.onload = (typeof window.onload != 'function') ?
            loadChartbeat : function() {
                oldonload();
                loadChartbeat();
            };
    })();
    </script>
    <div class="rebelbar-fake">
    </div>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         require(['jquery', 'underscore'], function($, _) {
		function spanAllLines( element  ){
			var padding= 5;
			var spanCSS= { "white-space": "nowrap", "display": "inline-block" };

			//check if the element where re-rendered before
			if ($(element).attr('rendered') != 'true'){
				$(element).attr('data-text', $(element).html());
				$(element).attr('rendered', 'true');
				//Adding css to current element
				$(element).css({ "display": "inline"});
			}

			var fullText= $(element).attr('data-text').split(' ');
			var fullWidth= $(element).parent().width()- (padding*2);//takes parent width, its the real full width
			var textLine= lastTextLine= ""; //we use an string, because append function add  break lines 
			var span= document.createElement('div');

			$(element).html(''); //clean all content

			$(element).append(span);
			$(element).children().css(spanCSS);

			for (key in fullText){
				textLine += fullText[key] + " ";
				$(span).html(textLine);
				if ($(span).width() &gt; fullWidth){
					$(span).html(lastTextLine);
					span = document.createElement('div');
					$(element).append(span);
					$(element).children().css( spanCSS );
					textLine = fullText[key] + " ";
					$(span).html(textLine);
				}
				lastTextLine= textLine;
			}
		}
		
		window.onresize= function(){ _.each($('.add-span') , spanAllLines); };
		_.each($('.add-span') , spanAllLines);
    });
        </script>

          <h1 class="headline">
           This Traffic Cop Loves His Job, And When You See Him Dance, You'll Love Him
          </h1>
         </div>
         <h2 class="subheadline">
          Ranjeet Singh is a traffic cop fromMadhya Pradesh, India, but he does much more than just direct traffic. He breaks out some serious moves in the middle of the street, including his own version of the "moonwalk." Ranjeet knows that many traffic cops are ignored, especially inMadhya Pradesh's chaotic streets, so he makes people
          <em>
           want
          </em>
          to listen to what he has to say. Just look at him workin' it!
         </h2>
